</p>
<ol><li><a href = vnd.unilang:enkelvoud.html>enkelvoud</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:verleden.html>verleden</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:tijd.html>tijd</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a>  <a href = vnd.unilang:posten.html>posten</a><br />

***poten.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:poten.html>poten</a> (3971)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">pōten</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*poton</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*putōną</i>.

<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:poten.html>poten</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li>to set, plant, place a young plant or large seed individually in soil or other substrate where it can grow; sow</li>
<li>to release young fish or <a href = vnd.unilang:halal.html>-</a> eggs to regulate the population for <a href = vnd.unilang:fishers.html>fishers</a>' benefit</li></ol>

<p>From dialectal <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:pot.html>pot</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">head</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, originally the word meant 'stubborn', it shifted meaning and <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> now analyzed as <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:poot.html>poot</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:leg.html>leg</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-ig</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:potig.html>potig</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:potig.html>potiger</a></b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl">potigst</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>rugged, vigorous, robust</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Inflection">Inflection</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Bijvoeglijk_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:bijvoeglijk.html>Bijvoeglijk</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:potig.html>potig</a></b>
</p>
<ol><li><a href = vnd.unilang:stevig.html>stevig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:uit.html>uit</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:kluiten.html>kluiten</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:gewassen.html>gewassen</a>, weerbaar, <a href = vnd.unilang:ruig.html>ruig</a>

<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:potje.html>potje</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">jar</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-s-</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:latijn.html>Latijn</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">Latin</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">medicine<span class="ib-comma">,</span> now historical</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> Latin used to label jars and bottles, originally to avoid confusion about the contents, but <a href = vnd.unilang:later.html>later</a> as a form of jargon.</li>

***potlood.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:potlood.html>potlood</a> (7438)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:pot.html>pot</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:pot.html>pot</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:lood.html>lood</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">lead</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Originally it <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> a name for graphite, used for glazing <a href = vnd.unilang:pots.html>pots</a>, which <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> misidentified as a form of lead. Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">black lead</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:potlood.html>potlood</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:potloden.html>potloden</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:potloodje.html>potloodje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>A pencil.</li>
<li>Graphite.
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:grafiet.html>grafiet</a></span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">especially</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> Graphite powder.</li></ol>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:potlood.html>potlood</a></b> <span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic"><a href = vnd.unilang:o.html>o</a></span>
</p>
<ol><li><span style="background-color:FFFFE0;font-style: italic;">(teken- <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> schrijfmateriaal)</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:schrijfgerei.html>schrijfgerei</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:met.html>met</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zachte.html>zachte</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:stift.html>stift</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:vervaardigd.html>vervaardigd</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:klei.html>klei</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:grafiet.html>grafiet</a> ingebed in <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:houten.html>houten</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:huls.html>huls</a>
<dl><dd><ul><li><i><a href = vnd.unilang:deze.html>Deze</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:tekening.html>tekening</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:met.html>met</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:potlood.html>potlood</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:gemaakt.html>gemaakt</a>.</i> </li></ul></dd></dl></li>

***potloodventer.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:potloodventer.html>potloodventer</a> (48657)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:potlood.html>potlood</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">pencil, euphemism for an erect <a href = vnd.unilang:penis.html>penis</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:venter.html>venter</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">salesman, vendor, <a href = vnd.unilang:hawker.html>hawker</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. The sense for an <a href = vnd.unilang:exhibitionist.html>exhibitionist</a> originated as a <a href = vnd.unilang:slang.html>slang</a> term among the Dutch police.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:potloodventer.html>potloodventer</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:potloodventers.html>potloodventers</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:potloodventer.html>potloodventertje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">somewhat humorous</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A male flasher, an <a href = vnd.unilang:exhibitionist.html>exhibitionist</a> who suddenly exposes his phallus. <span class="defdate">[from 1970s]</span>

***potpourri.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:potpourri.html>potpourri</a> (48656)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr"><a href = vnd.unilang:pot.html>pot</a> pourri</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:rotten.html>rotten</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:pot.html>pot</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, itself a calque from Spanish <i class="Latn mention" lang="es">olla podrida</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:potpourri.html>potpourri</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:potpourri.html>potpourri</a>'s</b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:potpourri.html>potpourrietje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>several <a href = vnd.unilang:songs.html>songs</a> strung together (<a href = vnd.unilang:medley.html>medley</a>).</li>
<li>A <span class="Latn" lang="en">mixture</span> of <span class="Latn" lang="en">dried</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en">fragrant</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en">plant</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en">material</span>, often in a <span class="Latn" lang="en">decorative</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en">bowl</span>, used to <span class="Latn" lang="en">scent</span> a <span class="Latn" lang="en">room</span>.</li>
<li>A number of varied literary articles.</li></ol>

***potverdorie.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:potverdorie.html>potverdorie</a> (18363)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Likely originating as a lengthening of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">potver</i>, a minced oath derived from <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:godver.html>godver</a></i>; alternatively analogically formed from <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:godverdorie.html>godverdorie</a></i>, but <i><a href = vnd.unilang:potverdorie.html>potverdorie</a></i> <a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>has</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:been.html>been</a> attested somewhat earlier, although this could be due to <i><a href = vnd.unilang:godverdorie.html>godverdorie</a></i> being more taboo.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Interjection">Interjection</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:potverdorie.html>potverdorie</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><a href = vnd.unilang:dang.html>dang</a>, darned <span class="defdate">[from 1890s]</span></li></ol>
<hr><h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Synoniemen"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:synoniemen.html>Synoniemen</a></i></span></h5>
<ul><li>verdikkeme, potverdikke, potverdikkeme, potdikkie, potjandorie, potjandosie, potjandrie, potverdrie, potverdriedubbeltjes, potverdomme, potdomme, <a href = vnd.unilang:verdorie.html>verdorie</a>, potdorie</li></ul>
</body> 
***potvis.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:potvis.html>potvis</a> (59564)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Compound of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:pot.html>pot</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:pot.html>pot</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:vis.html>vis</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">fish</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. The part <i><a href = vnd.unilang:pot.html>pot</a></i> refers to the sperm whale's blunt head due to its melon and spermaceti organ.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:potvis.html>potvis</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:potvissen.html>potvissen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:potvis.html>potvisje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>sperm whale, <i>Physeter catodon</i> (syn. <i>Physeter macrocephalus</i>)</li>
<li>sperm whale, any member of the family Physeteridae, including the above and several prehistoric species</li></ol>

***pover.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:pover.html>pover</a> (50928)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:pover.html>pover</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">povre</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la"><a href = vnd.unilang:pauper.html>pauper</a></i>. Cognate to <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">pauvre</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:pover.html>pover</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl">poverder</b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl">poverst</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="Latn" lang="en">poor</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">needy</span></li>

<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:dat.html>Dat</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:povere.html>povere</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:uitkomst.html>uitkomst</a>.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">That <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> an <b>unimpressive</b> result.</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***powwow.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:powwow.html>powwow</a> (46634)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From an <span class="etylcleanup"><span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Algonquian_languages" class="extiw" title="w:Algonquian languages">Algonquian</a></span></span> language, probably <span class="etylcleanup"><span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Massachusett_language" class="extiw" title="w:Massachusett language">Massachusett</a></span></span> <span class="Latn" lang="wam">pauwau</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">he uses divination; he practices magic or sorcery</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> or <span class="etylcleanup"><span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Narragansett_language" class="extiw" title="w:Narragansett language">Narragansett</a></span></span> <span class="Latn" lang="xnt">powwáw</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">sorcerer, shaman</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etylcleanup"><span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Algonquian" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Algonquian">Proto-Algonquian</a></span></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="alg-pro">*pawe·wa</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">one who <a href = vnd.unilang:dreams.html>dreams</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:powwow.html>powwow</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">powwows</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>A ritual conducted by a Native American shaman.</li>
<li>A Native American shaman.</li>
<li>A Native American council or meeting.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">informal</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A short, private conference.
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1913</b>,  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Joseph_C._Lincoln" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Joseph C. Lincoln">Joseph C. Lincoln</a>,  chapter 12, in  <cite><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://openlibrary.org/works/OL5535161W"><a href = vnd.unilang:mr.html>Mr</a>. Pratt's Patients</a></cite>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">While the <b><a href = vnd.unilang:powwow.html>powwow</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> going on the big woman <a href = vnd.unilang:came.html>came</a> back again. She <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> consider'ble rumpled and scratched up, but there <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> fire in her eye.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">Canada, US</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A large gathering during which Indigenous <a href = vnd.unilang:songs.html>songs</a> and <a href = vnd.unilang:dances.html>dances</a> are showcased for an audience, essentially a recital or concert.  Often also doubles as a fundraiser, or can be <a href = vnd.unilang:held.html>held</a> in conjunction with a non-indigneous fair or exhibition in order to attract a large crowd, as at the <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Calgary_Stampede" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Calgary Stampede">Calgary Stampede</a> and <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/K-Days" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:K-Days">K-Days</a>.</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:powwow.html>powwow</a></strong> (<i>third-person singular simple present</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en 3 | s | pres-form-of" lang="en">powwows</b>, <i>present participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en pres | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">powwowing</b>, <i>simple past and past participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en past | and | past | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">powwowed</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> of Native Americans</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To hold a meeting; to gather together in council.
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>2005</b>,  Glen <a href = vnd.unilang:tucker.html>Tucker</a>,  <cite>Tecumseh: A Vision of Glory</cite>, page 224:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">[The] Indians saw everything that happened and <b>powwowed</b> all night, needing more than anything else the presence of Tecumseh. The most aggressive element <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> the Winnebagos, who insisted on attacking.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> of Native Americans and by extension other groups, such as the Pennsylvania Dutch</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To conduct a ritual in which magic <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> used.
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>2007</b>,  David W. <a href = vnd.unilang:kriebel.html>Kriebel</a>,  <cite>Powwowing Among the Pennsylvania Dutch</cite>, page 10:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">Maybe no one— except possibly Leah— <b>powwowed</b> anymore.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">informal<span class="ib-comma">,</span> intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To hold a private conference.</li></ol>
</body>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_High_German" class="extiw" title="w:Middle High German">Middle High German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="gmh">praht</i>, southern variety of <i class="Latn mention" lang="gmh">braht</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_High_German" class="extiw" title="w:Old High German">Old High German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="goh">braht</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="goh">praht</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*brahtaz</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">cracking, snapping, noise</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. ***prairiehond.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:prairiehond.html>prairiehond</a> (43199)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">prairie</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">prairie, plain</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hond.html>hond</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">dog</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, calque of  <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">prairie dog</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:prairiehond.html>prairiehond</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:prairiehonden.html>prairiehonden</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:prairiehond.html>prairiehondje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">zoology</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> The burrowing rodent prairie dog, of the genus <i>Cynomys</i></li></ol>

***praktijk.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:praktijk.html>praktijk</a> (5692)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:praktijk.html>praktijk</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> or <abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:praktijken.html>praktijken</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>practice
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">uncountable</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> application of theory</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">countable</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> doing(s) of something</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">countable</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:clientèle.html>clientèle</a> (lawyer or doctor)</li></ol></li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>

<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:praktiseren.html>praktiseren</a></strong>
</p>

<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to observe (a tradition or religion), to practise</li></ol>

***prat.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:prat.html>prat</a> (37851)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_3">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Germanic, cognate with <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:praten.html>praten</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to talk</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:pret.html>pret</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">fun</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> and <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:prat.html>prat</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">trick, prank</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective_2">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:prat.html>prat</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:prat.html>pratter</a></b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl">pratst</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>(<i>used with <a href = vnd.unilang:op.html>op</a></i>) focused, <a href = vnd.unilang:bent.html>bent</a>, fixated</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">obsolete</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> proud, haughty, <a href = vnd.unilang:arrogant.html>arrogant</a></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Inflection">Inflection</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_4">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<ol><li>A pride, arrogance</li>
<li>the act of pouting or sulking</li></ol>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:prat.html>prat</a></b>

***praten.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:praten.html>praten</a> (192)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:praten.html>praten</a></i>, further etymology unknown. Cognates are found only in <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Low_German" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Low German">Middle Low German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="gml"><a href = vnd.unilang:praten.html>praten</a></i>. <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:prate.html>prate</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">prattle</i> and the various Scandinavian verbs <a href = vnd.unilang:were.html>were</a> borrowed from these two languages.
</p>

***precies.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:precies.html>precies</a> (329)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_French" class="extiw" title="w:Middle French">Middle French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="frm">precis</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">precisus</i>, from <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">praecīsus</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:precies.html>precies</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:preciezer.html>preciezer</a></b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:meest.html>meest</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:precies.html>precies</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl">preciest</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>exact, precise</li>
<li>accurate, careful</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Inflection">Inflection</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:precies.html>precies</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li>exactly, precisely</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Belgium" class="extiw" title="w:Belgium">Belgium</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> seemingly
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonyms:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:net.html>net</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:alsof.html>alsof</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:blijkbaar.html>blijkbaar</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:schijnbaar.html>schijnbaar</a></span></span></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl">'<a href = vnd.unilang:t.html>t</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>Is</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:hier.html>hier</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:precies.html>precies</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:feest.html>feest</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:halal.html>-</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:lotto.html>Lotto</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:gewonnen.html>gewonnen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ofzo.html>ofzo</a>?</i><dl><dd><small>(please add an English translation of this usage example)</small></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***precisie.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:precisie.html>precisie</a> (13544)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Ultimately from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">praecīsiō</i>, probably borrowed <a href = vnd.unilang:via.html>via</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_French" class="extiw" title="w:Middle French">Middle French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="frm">precision</i>. Synchronically formed as <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:precies.html>precies</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">precise</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:-ie.html>-ie</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">-ion, -y</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
